   BhG 11.1	Bhu 11.1
   arjuna uvāca	arjunaH uvAca

   yat tvayoktaṃ vacas tena moho 'yaṃ vigato mama ||1||	yat tvayA-uktam vacaH tena mohaH ayam vigataH mama ||1||
   śrīdharaḥ :	SrIDaraH :
   vibhūti-vaibhavaṃ procya kṛpayā parayā hariḥ |	viBUti--vEBavam procya kRpayA parayA hariH |

   śoka-nivṛttaye | paramaṃ paramātma-niṣṭhaṃ guhyaṃ gopyam api	Soka-nivRttaye | paramam paramAtma--nizWam guhyam gopyam api

   ekāṃśena sthito jagat iti viśvātmakaṃ pārameśvaraṃ rūpaṃ bhagavatābhihitaṃ	eka-aMSena sTitaH jagat iti viSva-Atmakam pArameSvaram rUpam BagavatA-aBihitam

   iti | mad-anugrahāya śoka-nivṛtty-upakārāya paramaṃ	iti | mad--anugrahAya Soka-nivRtty-upakArAya paramam
   niratiśaya-puruṣārtha-paryavasāyi guhyaṃ gopyaṃ yasmai kasmaicid vaktum	niratiSaya--puruza-arTa--paryavasAyi guhyam gopyam yasmE kasmEcid vaktum
   anarham api | adhyātma-saṃjñitam adhyātmam iti śabditam	anarham api | aDyAtma--saMjQitam aDyAtmam iti Sabditam

   ādi-ṣaṣṭhādhyāya-paryantaṃ tv apadārtha-pradhānaṃ yat tvayā	Adi-zazWa-aDyAya--paryantam tu apadArTa--praDAnam yat tvayA
   parama-kāruṇikena sarvajñenoktaṃ vaco vākyaṃ tena vākyenāham eṣāṃ hantā	parama-kAruNikena sarvajQena-uktam vacaH vAkyam tena vAkyena-aham ezAm hantA
   mayaite hanyanta ity ādivividha-viparyāsa-lakṣaṇo moho 'yam	mayA-ete hanyante iti Adi-viviDa--viparyAsa--lakzaNaH mohaH ayam
   anubhava-sākṣiko vigato vinaṣṭo mama | tatrāsakṛd ātmanaḥ	anuBava--sAkzikaH vigataH vinazwaH mama | tatra-asakRt AtmanaH
   sarva-vikriyā-śūnyatvokteḥ ||1||	sarva--vikriyA--SUnya-tva-ukteH ||1||
   viśvanāthaḥ :	viSvanATaH :
   ekādaśe viśvarūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā sambhrānta-dhīḥ stuvan |	ekAdaSe viSva-rUpam dRzwvA samBrAnta-DIH stuvan |

   pūrvādhyāyānte viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam ekāṃśena sthito jagat iti	pUrva-aDyAya-ante vizwaBya-aham idam kRtsnam eka-aMSena sTitaH jagat iti
   sarva-vibhūty-āśrayam ādi-puruṣaṃ sva-priya-sakhasyāṃśaṃ śrutvā	sarva--viBUti--ASrayam Adi-puruzam sva--priya--saKasya-aMSam SrutvA

   tad-vacaḥ | mohas tad-aiśvaryājñānam ||1||	tat--vacaH | mohaH tad--ESvarya-ajQAnam ||1||

   vibhūti-kathanopakrame viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam iti tad-upasaṃhāre ca	viBUti-kaTana-upakrame vizwaBya-aham idam kRtsnam iti tad--upasaMhAre ca
   nikhila-vibhūty-āśrayo mahat-sraṣṭā puruṣaḥ svasya kṛṣṇasyāvatāraḥ, sa tu	niKila--viBUti--ASrayaH mahat--srazwA puruzaH svasya kRzNasya-avatAraH, sa tu

   sakhyānanda-sindhu-nimagno 'rjunas tat-puruṣa-rūpaṃ didṛkṣuḥ kṛṣṇoktam	saKi-Ananda--sinDu--nimagnaH arjunaH tat--puruza-rUpam didRkzuH kRzNa-uktam

   vacas tvayoktaṃ tena mama mohaḥ kathaṃ vidyām ity-ādy-ukto vigato naṣṭaḥ |	vacaH tvayA-uktam tena mama mohaH kaTam vidyAm iti--Adi--uktaH vigataH nazwaH |
   adhyātmam ātmani paramātmani tvayi yā vibhūti-lakṣaṇā saṃjñā sā jātā |	aDyAtmam Atmani paramAtmani tvayi yA viBUti-lakzaNA saMjQA sA jAtAH |

   tvad-anyāgamyam ity arthaḥ ||1||	tvad--anya-agamyam iti arTaH ||1||
   BhG 11.2	Bhu 11.2
   bhavāpyayau hi bhūtānāṃ śrutau vistaraśo mayā |	Bava-apyayO hi BUtAnAm SrutO vistaraSaH mayA |
   tvattaḥ kamala-patrākṣa māhātmyam api cāvyayam ||2||	tvattaH kamala-patra-akza mAhAtmyam api ca-avyayam ||2||
   śrīdharaḥ : kiṃ ca bhavāpyayāv iti | bhūtānāṃ bhavāpyayau sṛṣṭi-pralayau	SrIDaraH : kim ca Bava-apyayO iti | BUtAnAm Bava-apyayO sRzwi--pralayO
   tvattaḥ sakāśād eva bhavataḥ | iti śrutaṃ mayā | ahaṃ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ	tvattaH sakASAt eva BavataH | iti Srutam mayA | aham kRtsnasya jagataH
   prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā ity ādau | vistaraśaḥ punaḥ punaḥ | kamalasya	praBavaH pralayaH taTA iti AdO | vistaraSaH punar punar | kamalasya
   patre iva suprasanne viśāle akṣiṇī yasya tava he kamala-patrākṣa !	patre iva su-prasanne viSAle akziNI yasya tava he kamala-patra-akzaH !

   sarva-niyantṛtve 'pi śubhāśubha-karma-kārayitṛtve 'pi	sarva--niyantR-tve api SuBa-aSuBa-karma-kArayitR-tve api

   avikārāvaidharmyāsaṅgaudāsīnyādi-lakṣaṇam aparimitaṃ mahattvaṃ ca śrutam -	avikAra-avEDarmya-asaFga-OdAsIni-Adi--lakzaNam aparimitam mahat-tvam ca Srutam -
   avyaktaṃ vyaktim āpannaṃ manyante mām abuddhayaḥ iti | mayā tatam idaṃ	avyaktam vyaktim Apannam manyante mAm abudDayaH iti | mayA tatam idam
   sarvam iti | na ca māṃ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti iti | samo 'haṃ	sarvam iti | na ca mAm tAni karmANi nibaDnanti iti | samaH aham
   sarva-bhūteṣu ity ādinā | atas tvat-paratantratvād api jīvānām ahaṃ	sarva-BUtezu iti AdinA | atas tu-at-para-tantra-tvAt api jIvAnAm aham
   kartety ādir madīyo moho vigata iti bhāvaḥ ||2||	kartA-iti AdiH madIyaH mohaH vigataH iti BAvaH ||2||
   madhusūdanaḥ : tathā saptamād ārabhya daśama-paryantaṃ	maDusUdanaH : taTA saptamAt AraBya daSama--paryantam
   tat-padārtha-nirṇaya-pradhānam api bhagavato vacanaṃ mayā śrutam ity āha	tat--padArTa--nirNaya--praDAnam api BagavataH vacanam mayA Srutam iti Aha
   bhavāpyayāv iti | bhūtānāṃ bhavāpyayāv utpatti-pralayau tvatta eva	Bava-apyayO iti | BUtAnAm Bava-apyayO utpatti-pralayO tvattaH eva
   bhavantau tvatta eva vistaraśo mayā śrutau na tu saṃkṣepeṇāsakṛd ity	BavantO tvattaH eva vistaraSaH mayA SrutO na tu saMkzepeNa-asakRt iti-
   arthaḥ | kamalasya patre iva dīrghe raktānte parama-manorame akṣiṇī yasya	arTaH | kamalasya patre iva dIrGe rakta-ante parama--manorame akziNI yasya
   tava sa tvaṃ he kamala-patrākṣa ! atisaundaryātiśayollekho 'yaṃ	tava sa tvam he kamala-patra-akza ! ati-sOndarya-atiSaya-ulleKaH ayam
   premātiśayāt | na kevalaṃ bhavāpyayau tvattaḥ śrutau mahātmanas tava bhāvo	prema-atiSayAt | na kevalam Bava-apyayO tvattaH SrutO mahAtmanaH tava BAvaH-
   māhātmyam atiśayaiśvaryaṃ viśva-sṛṣṭy-ādi-kartṛtve 'py avikāre tvaṃ	mAhAtmyam atiSaya-ESvaryam viSva--sRzwi--Adi-kartR-tve api avikAre tvam
   śubhāśubha-karma-kārayitṛtve 'py avaiṣamyaṃ	SuBa-aSuBa-karma-kArayitR-tve api avEzamyam
   bandha-mokṣādi-vicitra-phala-dātṛtve 'py asaṅgaudāsīnyam anyad api	banDa--mokza-Adi--vicitra--Pala--dAtR-tve api asaFga-OdAsInyam anyat api
   sarvātmatvādi sopādhikaṃ nirupādhikam api cāvyayam akṣayaṃ mayā śrutam iti	sarva-Atma-tva-Adi sa-upADikam nirupADikam api ca-avyayam akzayam mayA Srutam iti
   pariṇatam anuvartate ca-kārāt ||2||	pariNatam anuvartate ca-kArAt ||2||
   viśvanāthaḥ : asmin ṣaṭke tu bhavāpyayau sṛṣṭi-saṃhārau tvatta iti ahaṃ	viSvanATaH : asmin zawke tu Bava-apyayO sRzwi--saMhArO tvattaH iti aham
   kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā ity ādināvyayaṃ māhātmyaṃ	kRtsnasya jagataH praBavaH pralayaH taTA iti Adina-avyayam mAhAtmyam
   sṛṣṭy-ādi-kartṛtve 'py adhikārāsaṅgādi-lakṣaṇaṃ mayā tatam idaṃ sarvam iti	sRzwi--Adi-kartR-tve api aDikAra-AsaFga-Adi--lakzaNam mayA tatam idam sarvam iti
   na ca māṃ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti ity ādinā ||2||	na ca mAm tAni karmANi nibaDnanti iti AdinA ||2||
   baladevaḥ : kiṃ ca bhaveti | he kamala-patrākṣa ! kamala-patre ivātiramye	baladevaH : kim ca Bava-iti | he kamala-patra-akzaH ! kamala--patre iva-ati-ramye
   dīrgha-raktānte cākṣiṇī yasyeti premātiśayāt saundaryātiśayollekhaḥ |	dIrGa--rakta-ante ca-akziNI yasya-iti prema-atiSayAt sOndarya-atiSaya-ulleKaH |
   tvattas tvad-dhetukau bhūtānāṃ bhavāpyayau sarga-pralayau mayā tvattaḥ	tvattaH tvad--DetukO BUtAnAm Bava-apyayO sarga--pralayO mayA tvattaH

   tathā ity ādināvyayaṃ nityaṃ māhātmyam aiśvaryaṃ ca tava sarva-kartṛtve	taTA iti Adina-avyayam nityam mAhAtmyam ESvaryam ca tava sarva-kartR-tve
   'pi nirvikāratvaṃ sarva-niyantṛte 'py asaṅgatvam ity evam ādi tvatta eva	api nirvikAra-tvam sarva--niyantRte api asaFga-tvam iti evam Adi tvattaH eva
   mayā vistaraśaḥ śrutam mayā tatam idaṃ sarvam ity ādibhiḥ ||2||	mayA vistaraSaH Srutam mayA tatam idam sarvam iti AdiBiH ||2||
   BhG 11.3	Bhu 11.3
   evam etad yathāttha tvam ātmānaṃ parameśvara |	evam etat yaTA-AtTa tvam AtmAnam parameSvara |

   śrīdharaḥ : kiṃ ca evam etad iti | bhavāpyayau hi bhūtānām ity ādi mayā	SrIDaraH : kim ca evam etat iti | Bava-apyayO hi BUtAnAm iti Adi mayA
   śrutam | yathā cedānīm ātmānaṃ tvam āttha viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam	Srutam | yaTA ca-idAnIm AtmAnam tvam AtTa vizwaBya-aham idam kRtsnam
   ekāṃśena sthito jagat ity evaṃ kathayasi he parameśvara | evam eva tat |	eka-aMSena sTitaH jagat iti evam kaTayasi he parameSvara | evam eva tat |

   mahatī vartata iti sarvajñatvāt tvaṃ jānāsi sarvāntaryāmitvāc ceti	mahatI vartate iti sarvajQa-tvAt tvam jAnAsi sarva-antaryAmi-tvAt ca-iti
   sūcayati ||3||	sUcayati ||3||
   viśvanāthaḥ : idānīm ātmānaṃ tvam yathāttha viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ kṛtsnam	viSvanATaH : idAnIm AtmAnam tvam yaTA-AtTa vizwaBya-aham idam kRtsnam
   ekāṃśena sthito jagat iti, tac caivam eva mama nātra ko 'py aviśvāso	eka-aMSena sTitaH jagat iti, tat ca-evam eva mama na-atra kaH api aviSvAsaH-
   'stīti bhāvaḥ | kintu tad api saṃhṛtārtho bubhūṣayā tavaiśvaraṃ tad-rūpaṃ	asti-iti BAvaH | kintu tat api saMhRta-arTaH buBUzayA tava-ESvaram tat--rUpam
   draṣṭum icchāmi yenaikāṃśeneśvara-rūpeṇa tvaṃ jagat viṣṭabhya vartase |	drazwum icCAmi yena-eka-aMSena-ISvara--rUpeNa tvam jagat vizwaBya vartase |
   tasyaiva te rūpam aham idānīṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ draṣṭum icchāmīty arthaḥ ||3||	tasya-eva te rUpam aham idAnIm cakzurByAm drazwum icCAmi-iti arTaH ||3||
   baladevaḥ : evam iti viṣṭabhyāham idaṃ ity ādinā yathā tam ātmānaṃ svam	baladevaH : evam iti vizwaBya-aham idam iti AdinA yaTA tam AtmAnam svam
   āttha bravīṣi, tad etad evam eva na tava me saṃśaya-leśo 'pi tathāpi	AtTa bravIzi, tat etat evam eva na tava me saMSaya-leSaH api taTA-api
   tavaiśvaraṃ sarva-praśāstṛ tad-rūpam ahaṃ kautukād draṣṭum icchāmi | he	tava-ESvaram sarva-praSAstR tad--rUpam aham kOtukAt drazwum icCAmi | he
   parameśvara he puruṣottameti sambodhayan mama tad-didṛkṣāṃ jānāsy eva |	parameSvara he puruzottamA-iti samboDayan mama tad--didRkzAm jAnAsi eva |

   BhG 11.4	Bhu 11.4

   śrīmad-bhagavad-gītā-gūḍhārtha-dīpikāyām viśva-rūpa-darśana-nirūpaṇaṃ nāma	SrImat--Bagavat--gItA-gUXa-arTa-dIpikAyAm viSva-rUpa-darSana-nirUpaNam nAma
   ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||	ekAdaSaH aDyAyaH ||
   viśvanāthaḥ : atha bhakti-prakaraṇopasaṃhārārthaṃ saptamādhyāyādiṣu ye ye	viSvanATaH : aTa Bakti-prakaraNa-upasaMhAra-arTam saptama-aDyAya-Adizu ye ye
   bhaktā uktās teṣāṃ sāmānya-lakṣaṇam āha mat-karma-kṛd iti | saṅga-varjitaḥ	BaktAH uktAH tezAm sAmAnya--lakzaNam Aha mat--karma--kRt iti | saFga--varjitaH
   saṅga-rahitaḥ ||55||	saFga--rahitaH ||55||
   kṛṣṇasyaiva mahaiśvaryaṃ mamaivāsmin raṇe jayaḥ |	kRzNasya-eva mahA-ESvaryam mama-eva-asmin raNe jayaH |
   ity arjuno niścikāyety-adhyāyārtho nirūpitaḥ ||	iti arjunaH niScikAya-iti--aDyAya-arTaH nirUpitaH ||
   iti sārārtha-varṣiṇyāṃ harṣiṇyāṃ bhakta-cetasām |	iti sAra-arTa-varziNyAm harziNyAm Bakta--cetasAm |
   gītāsv ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||11||	gItAsu ekAdaSaH aDyAyaH saFgataH saFgataH satAm ||11||
   baladevaḥ : atha sva-prāpti-karīm ananyāṃ bhaktim upadiśann upasaṃharati	baladevaH : aTa sva--prApti-karIm ananyAm Baktim upadiSan upasaMharati
   mad iti | mat-sambandhinī	mat iti | mat--sambanDinI
   man-mandira-nirmāṇa-tad-vimārjana-mat-puṣpa-bāṭī-tulasī-kānana-saṃskāra-tat-sevanādīni	man-mandira--nirmANa--tad--vimArjana--mat--puzpa-bAwI--tula-sI-kAnana--saMskAra---tat--sevana-AdIni
   karmādīni karotīti mat-karma-kṛt | mat-paramo mām eva na tu svargādikaṃ	karma-AdIni karoti-iti mat--karma-kRt | mat--paramaH mAm eva na tu svarga-Adikam
   sva-pumarthaṃ jānan | mad-bhakto	sva-pum-arTam jAnan | mad-BaktaH-
   mac-chravaṇādi-nava-vidha-bhakti-rasa-nirataḥ | saṅga-varjito	mac--SravaNa-Adi-nava-viDa--Bakti-rasa--nirataH | saFga--varjitaH-
   mad-vimukha-saṃsargam asahamānaḥ | sarva-bhūteṣu nirvairaḥ | teṣv api	mad--vimuKa--saMsargam asahamAnaH | sarva-BUtezu nirvEraH | tezu api
   mad-vimukheṣu pratikūleṣu satsu vaira-śūnyaḥ | sva-kleśasya	mad--vimuKezu pratikUlezu satsu vEra--SUnyaH | sva--kleSasya
   sva-pūrvakarma-nimittakatva-vimarśena teṣu vaira-nimittābhāvāt | evambhūto	sva-pUrva-karma--nimittaka-tva--vimarSena tezu vEra--nimitta-aBAvAt | evamBUtaH-
   yo māṃ narākāraṃ kṛṣṇam eti labhate, nānyaḥ ||55||	yaH mAm nara-AkAram kRzNam eti laBate, na-anyaH ||55||
   pūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇo 'vatāritvāt tad-bhaktānāṃ jayo raṇe |	pUrNaH kRzNaH avatAri-tvAt tad--BaktAnAm jayaH raNe |
   bhārate pāṇḍu-putrāṇām ity ekādaśa-nirṇayaḥ ||	BArate pANxu-putrANAm iti ekAdaSa--nirNayaH ||
